Registration Patterns\\n\\n## Overview\\nAcross the three analyzed repositories (Kubernetes, Prometheus, and Grafana), three distinct patterns emerge for Prometheus metric registration and exposure, each suited to different architectural contexts.\\n\\n## 1. Kubernetes Pattern: Wrapped Registry with Stability Framework\\n\\n**Key Files:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go`: Global registry facade\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`: Custom kubeRegistry wrapper\\n\\n**Pattern Description:**\\nKubernetes implements a stability-aware registry layer that wraps the Prometheus client library. The key innovation is the `kubeRegistry` type that extends a base `PromRegistry` interface.\\n\\n**Registration Flow:**\\n1. Package-level metric definitions using Kubernetes-wrapped metric types (e.g., `metrics.NewCounterVec`)\\n2. Metrics registered via `init()` functions calling `legacyregistry.MustRegister()`\\n3. The `kubeRegistry` wraps each collector and checks if it should be created based on Kubernetes version (stability versioning)\\n4. Hidden/deprecated metrics are filtered out during registration via `Create()` method\\n5. The global `defaultRegistry = metrics.NewKubeRegistry()` is initialized in legacyregistry.go\\n\\n**Core Symbols:**\\n- `MustRegister()` (legacyregistry): Facade function that calls `defaultRegistry.MustRegister()`\\n- `NewKubeRegistry()`: Factory for creating a new wrapped registry\\n- `CustomMustRegister()`: Variant for custom stable collectors\\n- `RawMustRegister()`: Bypasses stability checks for native Prometheus collectors\\n\\n**Example Usage (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/metrics.go):**\\n```go\\nvar (\\n    eventCounter = metrics.NewCounterVec(...)\\n    errorCounter = metrics.NewCounterVec(...)\\n)\\nfunc init() {\\n    legacyregistry.MustRegister(eventCounter)\\n    legacyregistry.MustRegister(errorCounter)\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## 2. Prometheus Pattern: Optional Registerer Parameter with Conditional Registration\\n\\n**Key Files:**\\n- `cmd/prometheus/main.go`: Global metrics initialization\\n- `tsdb/db.go`: Database metrics with registerer parameter\\n- `scrape/metrics.go`: Scrape manager metrics factory\\n- `rules/group.go`: Rule group metrics factory\\n- `web/web.go`: Web handler metrics\\n\\n**Pattern Description:**\\nPrometheus uses a flexible pattern where metrics are created in factory functions that optionally accept a `prometheus.Registerer` parameter. If a registerer is provided (not nil), metrics are registered with it; otherwise, they're created but not registered.\\n\\n**Registration Flow:**\\n1. Global metrics defined at package level using `prometheus.NewCounter()`, `prometheus.NewHistogram()`, etc.\\n2. Global metrics registered in `init()` functions via `prometheus.MustRegister()`\\n3. Factory functions that create metric sets take `prometheus.Registerer` as optional parameter\\n4. Inside factory functions: check `if reg != nil` before calling `reg.MustRegister(...)`\\n5. This allows metrics to be registered with custom or nil registerers\\n\\n**Core Symbols:**\\n- `prometheus.MustRegister()`: Global registration with default registerer\\n- `NewDBMetrics()`: Factory returning *dbMetrics with registerer-aware registration\\n- `newScrapeMetrics()`: Factory for scrape pool metrics with optional registerer\\n- `NewGroupMetrics()`: Factory for rule group metrics with optional registerer\\n\\n**Example Usage (tsdb/db.go, lines 450-491):**\\n```go\\nfunc NewDBMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer) *dbMetrics {\\n    m := &dbMetrics{\\n        loadedBlocks: prometheus.NewGauge(...),\\n        reloads: prometheus.NewCounter(...),\\n        // ... more metrics\\n    }\\n    if r != nil {\\n        r.MustRegister(\\n            m.loadedBlocks,\\n            m.reloads,\\n            // ... register all metrics\\n        )\\n    }\\n    return m\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## 3. Grafana Pattern: promauto with Parameterized Registry\\n\\n**Key Files:**\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go`: Global promauto metrics\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go`: Custom metrics struct with manual registration\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/scheduler.go`: promauto.With() pattern\\n- `pkg/util/scheduler/queue.go`: Queue metrics with parameterized registerer\\n\\n**Pattern Description:**\\nGrafana uses the `promauto` package which automatically registers metrics with a registerer (either the default or a provided one). This eliminates the need for explicit `MustRegister()` calls.\\n\\n**Registration Flow:**\\n1. **Global Metrics** (auto-register to default):\\n   - `promauto.NewCounterVec()`, `promauto.NewHistogramVec()`, etc.\\n   - Automatically registers with `prometheus.DefaultRegisterer`\\n   - No explicit registration needed\\n\\n2. **Parameterized Metrics** (register to custom registerer):\\n   - `promauto.With(registerer).NewCounterVec()`\\n   - Automatically registers with the provided registerer\\n   - Used in factory functions taking `prometheus.Registerer` parameter\\n\\n3. **Manual Metrics Struct** Pattern:\\n   - Define metrics in a struct with field registerer\\n   - Implement `Register()` method that iterates collectors and calls `registry.Register()`\\n   - Implement `MustRegister()` as wrapper around `Register()` that panics on error\\n   - Allow chaining with `WithMustRegister()` method\\n\\n**Core Symbols:**\\n- `promauto.NewCounterVec()`: Auto-registers with default registerer\\n- `promauto.With(reg).NewCounterVec()`: Auto-registers with provided registerer\\n- `promauto.NewGaugeVec()`, `promauto.NewHistogramVec()`: Other metric types\\n- `NewSchedulerMetrics()`: Factory function accepting registerer parameter\\n- `PrometheusMetrics.MustRegister()`: Manual registration method\\n\\n**Example Usage (pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/scheduler.go, lines 38-70):**\\n```go\\nfunc NewSchedulerMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer) *Scheduler {\\n    return &Scheduler{\\n        Registerer: r,\\n        BehindSeconds: promauto.With(r).NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{...}),\\n        EvalTotal: promauto.With(r).NewCounterVec(\\n            prometheus.CounterOpts{...},\\n            []string{\\\"org\\\"},\\n        ),\\n        // ... more metrics auto-registered via promauto.With(r)\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Example Usage (pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go, lines 49-54):**\\n```go\\nfunc (m *PrometheusMetrics) MustRegister(registry prometheus.Registerer) {\\n    if err := m.Register(registry); err != nil {\\n        panic(err)\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## Comparative Analysis\\n\\n### Registration Mechanism\\n- **Kubernetes**: Wrapped, centralized registry with stability versioning; uses `legacyregistry.MustRegister()`\\n- **Prometheus**: Direct Prometheus library with optional registerer parameters; conditional registration pattern\\n- **Grafana**: promauto automatic registration; supports both global and parameterized modes\\n\\n### Flexibility\\n- **Kubernetes**: Least flexible (enforces versioning); best for large distributed systems with compatibility concerns\\n- **Prometheus**: Most flexible (optional registration); allows component-level metric management\\n- **Grafana**: Moderately flexible (auto-registration reduces boilerplate); good balance between simplicity and control\\n\\n### Metric Definition Location\\n- **Kubernetes**: Package-level variables with explicit registration in init()\\n- **Prometheus**: Package-level globals (global metrics) + factory functions (component-specific metrics)\\n- **Grafana**: Mix of package-level with promauto (global) and struct fields with factory functions (component-specific)\\n\\n### Registry Lifecycle\\n- **Kubernetes**: Single global kubeRegistry initialized once\\n- **Prometheus**: Default global registry + optional custom registries per component\\n- **Grafana**: Default global registry + custom registries passed as function parameters\\n\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6169,"cache_read_input_tokens":83940,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":6169},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"09ecaab7-238b-456e-ae8e-ce617085db90","uuid":"0f771a24-d464-4f23-ac7f-6ddccf073978"}

Registration Patterns\\n\\n## Overview\\nAcross the three analyzed repositories (Kubernetes, Prometheus, and Grafana), three distinct patterns emerge for Prometheus metric registration and exposure, each suited to different architectural contexts.\\n\\n## 1. Kubernetes Pattern: Wrapped Registry with Stability Framework\\n\\n**Key Files:**\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go`: Global registry facade\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`: Custom kubeRegistry wrapper\\n\\n**Pattern Description:**\\nKubernetes implements a stability-aware registry layer that wraps the Prometheus client library. The key innovation is the `kubeRegistry` type that extends a base `PromRegistry` interface.\\n\\n**Registration Flow:**\\n1. Package-level metric definitions using Kubernetes-wrapped metric types (e.g., `metrics.NewCounterVec`)\\n2. Metrics registered via `init()` functions calling `legacyregistry.MustRegister()`\\n3. The `kubeRegistry` wraps each collector and checks if it should be created based on Kubernetes version (stability versioning)\\n4. Hidden/deprecated metrics are filtered out during registration via `Create()` method\\n5. The global `defaultRegistry = metrics.NewKubeRegistry()` is initialized in legacyregistry.go\\n\\n**Core Symbols:**\\n- `MustRegister()` (legacyregistry): Facade function that calls `defaultRegistry.MustRegister()`\\n- `NewKubeRegistry()`: Factory for creating a new wrapped registry\\n- `CustomMustRegister()`: Variant for custom stable collectors\\n- `RawMustRegister()`: Bypasses stability checks for native Prometheus collectors\\n\\n**Example Usage (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/audit/metrics.go):**\\n```go\\nvar (\\n    eventCounter = metrics.NewCounterVec(...)\\n    errorCounter = metrics.NewCounterVec(...)\\n)\\nfunc init() {\\n    legacyregistry.MustRegister(eventCounter)\\n    legacyregistry.MustRegister(errorCounter)\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## 2. Prometheus Pattern: Optional Registerer Parameter with Conditional Registration\\n\\n**Key Files:**\\n- `cmd/prometheus/main.go`: Global metrics initialization\\n- `tsdb/db.go`: Database metrics with registerer parameter\\n- `scrape/metrics.go`: Scrape manager metrics factory\\n- `rules/group.go`: Rule group metrics factory\\n- `web/web.go`: Web handler metrics\\n\\n**Pattern Description:**\\nPrometheus uses a flexible pattern where metrics are created in factory functions that optionally accept a `prometheus.Registerer` parameter. If a registerer is provided (not nil), metrics are registered with it; otherwise, they're created but not registered.\\n\\n**Registration Flow:**\\n1. Global metrics defined at package level using `prometheus.NewCounter()`, `prometheus.NewHistogram()`, etc.\\n2. Global metrics registered in `init()` functions via `prometheus.MustRegister()`\\n3. Factory functions that create metric sets take `prometheus.Registerer` as optional parameter\\n4. Inside factory functions: check `if reg != nil` before calling `reg.MustRegister(...)`\\n5. This allows metrics to be registered with custom or nil registerers\\n\\n**Core Symbols:**\\n- `prometheus.MustRegister()`: Global registration with default registerer\\n- `NewDBMetrics()`: Factory returning *dbMetrics with registerer-aware registration\\n- `newScrapeMetrics()`: Factory for scrape pool metrics with optional registerer\\n- `NewGroupMetrics()`: Factory for rule group metrics with optional registerer\\n\\n**Example Usage (tsdb/db.go, lines 450-491):**\\n```go\\nfunc NewDBMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer) *dbMetrics {\\n    m := &dbMetrics{\\n        loadedBlocks: prometheus.NewGauge(...),\\n        reloads: prometheus.NewCounter(...),\\n        // ... more metrics\\n    }\\n    if r != nil {\\n        r.MustRegister(\\n            m.loadedBlocks,\\n            m.reloads,\\n            // ... register all metrics\\n        )\\n    }\\n    return m\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## 3. Grafana Pattern: promauto with Parameterized Registry\\n\\n**Key Files:**\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go`: Global promauto metrics\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go`: Custom metrics struct with manual registration\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/scheduler.go`: promauto.With() pattern\\n- `pkg/util/scheduler/queue.go`: Queue metrics with parameterized registerer\\n\\n**Pattern Description:**\\nGrafana uses the `promauto` package which automatically registers metrics with a registerer (either the default or a provided one). This eliminates the need for explicit `MustRegister()` calls.\\n\\n**Registration Flow:**\\n1. **Global Metrics** (auto-register to default):\\n   - `promauto.NewCounterVec()`, `promauto.NewHistogramVec()`, etc.\\n   - Automatically registers with `prometheus.DefaultRegisterer`\\n   - No explicit registration needed\\n\\n2. **Parameterized Metrics** (register to custom registerer):\\n   - `promauto.With(registerer).NewCounterVec()`\\n   - Automatically registers with the provided registerer\\n   - Used in factory functions taking `prometheus.Registerer` parameter\\n\\n3. **Manual Metrics Struct** Pattern:\\n   - Define metrics in a struct with field registerer\\n   - Implement `Register()` method that iterates collectors and calls `registry.Register()`\\n   - Implement `MustRegister()` as wrapper around `Register()` that panics on error\\n   - Allow chaining with `WithMustRegister()` method\\n\\n**Core Symbols:**\\n- `promauto.NewCounterVec()`: Auto-registers with default registerer\\n- `promauto.With(reg).NewCounterVec()`: Auto-registers with provided registerer\\n- `promauto.NewGaugeVec()`, `promauto.NewHistogramVec()`: Other metric types\\n- `NewSchedulerMetrics()`: Factory function accepting registerer parameter\\n- `PrometheusMetrics.MustRegister()`: Manual registration method\\n\\n**Example Usage (pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/scheduler.go, lines 38-70):**\\n```go\\nfunc NewSchedulerMetrics(r prometheus.Registerer) *Scheduler {\\n    return &Scheduler{\\n        Registerer: r,\\n        BehindSeconds: promauto.With(r).NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{...}),\\n        EvalTotal: promauto.With(r).NewCounterVec(\\n            prometheus.CounterOpts{...},\\n            []string{\\\"org\\\"},\\n        ),\\n        // ... more metrics auto-registered via promauto.With(r)\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Example Usage (pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go, lines 49-54):**\\n```go\\nfunc (m *PrometheusMetrics) MustRegister(registry prometheus.Registerer) {\\n    if err := m.Register(registry); err != nil {\\n        panic(err)\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n## Comparative Analysis\\n\\n### Registration Mechanism\\n- **Kubernetes**: Wrapped, centralized registry with stability versioning; uses `legacyregistry.MustRegister()`\\n- **Prometheus**: Direct Prometheus library with optional registerer parameters; conditional registration pattern\\n- **Grafana**: promauto automatic registration; supports both global and parameterized modes\\n\\n### Flexibility\\n- **Kubernetes**: Least flexible (enforces versioning); best for large distributed systems with compatibility concerns\\n- **Prometheus**: Most flexible (optional registration); allows component-level metric management\\n- **Grafana**: Moderately flexible (auto-registration reduces boilerplate); good balance between simplicity and control\\n\\n### Metric Definition Location\\n- **Kubernetes**: Package-level variables with explicit registration in init()\\n- **Prometheus**: Package-level globals (global metrics) + factory functions (component-specific metrics)\\n- **Grafana**: Mix of package-level with promauto (global) and struct fields with factory functions (component-specific)\\n\\n### Registry Lifecycle\\n- **Kubernetes**: Single global kubeRegistry initialized once\\n- **Prometheus**: Default global registry + optional custom registries per component\\n- **Grafana**: Default global registry + custom registries passed as function parameters\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
